if (!is_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') != 'e56aa97679c8421f69c146cf9119db882b9182bb') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== 'e56aa97679c8421f69c146cf9119db882b9182bb') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== 'b28f67a6be578a11d91a0752011e0708edd665a1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== 'e56aa97679c8421f69c146cf9119db882b9182bb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != '0d8811840a32626eef58eafc39837ee630251fdf') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '0d8811840a32626eef58eafc39837ee630251fdf') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '81027acf1aae61de105c077ae373828015b9bfda') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '0d8811840a32626eef58eafc39837ee630251fdf') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}
